	<header class="entry-header">
		<h1 class="entry-title">Berserk</h1>	</header><!-- .entry-header -->

	<div class="entry-content">
		
<div class="wp-block-media-text is-stacked-on-mobile" style="grid-template-columns:35% auto"><figure class="wp-block-media-text__media"><img class="aligncenter" fetchpriority="low" decoding="async" width="400" height="600" src="https://theberserk.online/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/Berserk.jpg" alt="Berserk manga" class="wp-image-1423 size-medium" srcset="https://theberserk.online/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/Berserk.jpg 400w, https://theberserk.online/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/Berserk-200x300.jpg 200w" sizes="auto"  loading="lazy"/></figure><div class="wp-block-media-text__content">
<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-fixed-layout"><tbody><tr><td><strong>Alternate Name(s)</strong></td><td><strong>ベルセルク (Japanese) ; 剑风传奇 (Simplified Chinese) ; 烙印勇士 (Traditional Chinese); Berserk (English) ;</strong></td></tr><tr><td><strong>Author</strong></td><td>MIURA Kentaro</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Genres</strong></td><td>Action, Adventure, Fantasy, Horror, Mature, Seinen, Supernatural, Tragedy</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Type</strong></td><td>Manga</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Realised in</strong></td><td>1988</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Status</strong></td><td>Ongoing</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
</div></div>



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table><tbody><tr><th colspan="2"><strong>«&nbsp;</strong>Synopsis&nbsp;<strong>»</strong></th></tr><tr><td colspan="2">Guts, known as the Black Swordsman, seeks sanctuary from the demonic forces attracted to him and his woman because of a demonic mark on their necks, and also vengeance against the man who branded him as an unholy sacrifice. Aided only by his titanic strength gained from a harsh childhood lived with mercenaries, a gigantic sword, and an iron prosthetic left hand, Gats must struggle against his bleak destiny, all the while fighting with a rage that might strip him of his humanity.</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>

			<div class="container">
				<div class="footer-widget-single">
					<div class="footer-widgets"><h3>About</h3>			<div class="textwidget"><p><i><b>Berserk</b></i> (Japanese: <span lang="ja">ベルセルク</span>, Hepburn: <span title="Hepburn transliteration"><i lang="ja-Latn">Beruseruku</i></span>) is a Japanese manga series written and illustrated by Kentaro Miura. Set in a medieval Europe-inspired dark fantasy world, the story centers on the characters of Guts, a lone swordsman, and Griffith, the leader of a mercenary band called the &#8220;Band of the Hawk&#8221;. The series follows Guts&#8217; journey seeking revenge on Griffith, who betrayed him and sacrificed his comrades to become a powerful demonic being.</p>
